; the line. If the line begins with ;^, then it is an optional string,
; and you should only modify that line if the definition in [common]
; is not accurate for that context.
; You can enlarge windows using 5CA1E00000000000=scale, for example:
;     [sws_DLG_109] ; IDD_ABOUT
;     5CA1E00000000000=1.2
; This makes the about box 1.2x wider than default.
; Do not change action tags like SWS:, SWS/S&M:, etc (such strings
; would be ignored).
; Once translated, the SWS LangPack has to be merged with the main REAPER one:
; see http://forum.cockos.com/showpost.php?p=941893&postcount=810.
